Operating income in the quarter was $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">126.7 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;as compared to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">143.7 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the same period of 2014. Excluding $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">15.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of restructuring and related costs, operating income was essentially flat year over year </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 31.1% and included a discrete benefit recorded in the quarter. The effective tax rate reported in the second quarter of 2014 was 33.4%. Net income in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">80.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">90.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;reported in the comparable period of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Earnings per diluted share for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;were $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1.37</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1.51</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;reported in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Excluding restructuring and related costs, earnings per diluted share increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1.56</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt"> (1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.  Free cash flow (defined as cash flow from operations less capital expenditures) was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$54.7 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;versus </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$43.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;reported in the comparable period of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font -</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">1</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">-</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1.7 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, an increase of </font><font Operating income was $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">231.7</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;million compared to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">248.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;million for the comparable period of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, and included $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">20.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of restructuring and related costs </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The effective tax rate in the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;months of 2015 was 32.0% and included a discrete benefit recorded in the second quarter. This compares to an effective tax rate of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">32.9%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;reported in the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Net income in the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">142.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;million compared to the $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">154.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;million for the comparable period of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Earnings per diluted share were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$2.44</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$2.59</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;reported for the comparable period of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Excluding restructuring and related costs, earnings per diluted share were $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2.68</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Free cash flow was $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">64.2</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;million compared to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">74.1</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;million reported in the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;months of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:16px;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><a name="sC21BADCD94C75A619FF3EA4B1153E7B3"></a><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">OPERATIONS REVIEW</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:16px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">David G. Nord, Chairman, President and Chief Executive Officer, said, &#8220;End market performance was mixed across Hubbell&#8217;s businesses during the second quarter. Organic growth was 1%, driven by solid non-residential and residential construction markets as well as stable utility demand. This sales growth was partially offset by weakness in energy markets and related slowing in industrial markets.&#8221; Mr. Nord continued, &#8220;Our sales composition impacted profit: lower margin businesses outgrew higher margin businesses and most of the sales growth came from acquisitions, which typically have lower margins in their first year. The favorable net impact of pricing, cost and productivity helped mitigate the mix headwind." Mr. Nord added, "And our Power segment delivered strong top line growth, driven by telecommunications, and incremental margins.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:16px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">"The cost reduction initiatives started late last year continue to gain traction. We have exited seven facilities and initiated actions that we expect will impact more than 250 positions across the company. These actions increased meaningfully in the second quarter as we responded to weakness in industrial markets and continued implementing projects to gain efficiencies in footprint and processes,&#8221; Mr. Nord stated. "Our model of supplementing market growth with acquisitions while increasing productivity remains intact as we improve our cost structure to enable future earnings growth. Further, we have leadership in place with operating expertise to execute this long-term vision; in May, we announced three Group Presidents - Kevin Poyck, Rodd Ruland and Darrin Wegman - supporting our Electrical segment, while Gary Amato remains Executive Vice President, Electrical Segment and Gerben Bakker continues to lead our Power segment." </font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Page -</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">2</font><font </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:16px;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Electrical segment net sales in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Acquisitions added 2% to net sales in the quarter while the unfavorable impact of foreign currency translation reduced sales by 2%. Organic volume increased slightly due to higher shipments in businesses exposed to the non-residential and residential markets partially offset by lower shipments in industrial and energy-related businesses. Operating income was $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">74.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">12.1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of net sales compared to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">95.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">15.6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of net sales, in the same period of 2014. Excluding restructuring and related costs, operating income was $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">87.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">14.3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of net sales </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Excluding restructuring and related costs, these decreases were primarily due to product and business mix headwind</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.  </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:16px;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Hubbell&#8217;s Power segment net sales in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">259.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">243.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;reported in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Acquisitions added 4% to net sales in the quarter while foreign currency translation reduced net sales by 1%. Organic sales increased 3% primarily due to increased shipments of telecommunications products. Compared to the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, operating income increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">8%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">52.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or 40 basis points to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">20.2%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of net sales. Excluding restructuring and related costs, operating income increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">13%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and margin expanded </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">130</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;basis points </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Both increases were primarily due to the favorable net impact of pricing, cost and productivity. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Page -</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">3</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">-</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sDA5EFAD2C3435F3FB82A759C7E417E8B"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">SUMMARY&#160;&amp; OUTLOOK</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:16px;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Mr. Nord commented,</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8220;Turning to the full year outlook, we expect strength in non-residential construction, modest growth of utility, and weakness in energy markets to continue; however, given current market trends and third-party forecasts, we are reducing our expectations of full year industrial growth to 0% to 2% and residential growth to 5% to 6%." Mr. Nord added, "We anticipate acquisitions will contribute approximately 4% to our net sales and foreign exchange will reduce our net sales by about 1%. Consequently, we are lowering our expectation for 2015 total net sales growth to approximately 3% to 4% from 5% to 7%.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:16px;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">"In response to end market conditions and, more generally, opportunities identified to reduce costs, we currently anticipate our restructuring and related actions to be approximately $0.45 per diluted share for the year, up from $0.25 previously. We are also increasing our expectation for full year share repurchases to approximately $150 million,&#8221; Mr. Nord continued. &#8220;Due to lower sales, the impact of unfavorable mix, and more cost reduction initiatives, we now expect earnings per diluted share in the range of $4.95 to $5.15 for 2015.&#8221; Mr. Nord concluded, &#8220;I remain enthusiastic about the prospects for Hubbell&#8217;s future shareholder value creation, as we take action to better position the Company for profitable sales growth over the long term."</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Certain statements contained herein may constitute forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. With </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;revenues of $3.4 billion, Hubbell Incorporated operates manufacturing facilities in the United States, Canada, Switzerland, Puerto Rico, Mexico, the People&#8217;s Republic of China (&#8220;China&#8221;), Italy, the United Kingdom, Brazil and Australia. Hubbell also participates in joint ventures in Taiwan and Hong Kong, and maintains sales offices in Singapore, China, India, Mexico, South Korea and countries in the Middle East. style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">HUBBELL INCORPORATED</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Footnotes</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">(1)  </sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">In order to provide a comparison that we believe provides more useful information regarding our underlying performance from period to period and to allow readers to assess the impact of restructuring activities and business transformation initiatives on our results of operations, the Company refers to earnings per diluted share, net income available to Hubbell common shareholders, and operating income, each excluding restructuring and related costs. Restructuring costs support our cost reduction efforts involving the consolidation of manufacturing and distribution facilities and workforce reductions. Restructuring related costs are one-time costs associated with our business transformation initiatives, including the consolidation of back-office functions and streamlining our processes. Each of these measures that exclude restructuring and related costs are non-GAAP measures. Reconciliations of these non-GAAP measures to the most directly comparable GAAP measure can be found in the Earnings Per Share Calculation and Segment Information tables within this press release.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">(2)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">Restructuring and related costs is a non-GAAP measure that we believe is useful to assess the impact of restructuring activities and business transformation initiatives on our operating results. Restructuring costs are incurred to support our cost reduction efforts involving the consolidation of manufacturing and distribution facilities and workforce reductions. Restructuring related costs are one-time costs associated with our business transformation initiatives, including the consolidation of back-office functions and streamlining our processes. Restructuring and related costs recognized in Cost of goods sold for the three months ended June 30, 2015 includes restructuring costs of $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">5.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;in the Electrical segment. For the six months ended June 30, 2015, restructuring and related costs recognized in Cost of goods sold include restructuring costs of $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">7.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;in the Electrical segment and $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">0.7 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;in the Power segment.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">(3)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;Restructuring and related costs recognized in Selling &amp; administrative expenses for the three months ended June 30, 2015 includes restructuring costs of $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">3.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;in the Electrical segment and $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">0.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;in the Power segment. For the six months ended June 30, 2015, restructuring and related costs recognized in Selling &amp; administrative expenses include restructuring costs of $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">3.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;in the Electrical segment and $</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">0.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">&#32;in the Power segment.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">(4)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">Net debt to total capital is a non-GAAP measure we believe is a useful measure for evaluating the Company's financial leverage and the ability to meet its funding needs.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">(5) </sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;">Free cash flow is a non-GAAP measure that we believe provides useful information regarding the Company's ability to generate cash without reliance on external financings. In addition, management uses free cash flow to evaluate the resources available for investments in the business, strategic acquisitions and further strengthening the balance sheet.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Page -</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">13</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">-</font></div></div>	</body>
